< review>
I reserved a unit a couple of weeks before I needed it.  Unfortunately, the unit size I had reserved was not available when I showed up.  The staff was able to offer me a bigger unit at a great rate as an alternative.  I had never stored at a facility like this so it took some time to "get it" on how storage works in the city.  They have carts available for use, loading docks, freight elevators, and drive-in options for cars and mid-sized trucks.

My only concerns regarding this facility (and the reason for 4 stars and not 5) is that my access card did not allow me to exit the underground drive-in area with my card,  I had to use the call box each time.  It is a glitch with their system and I will update this review if the issue gets resolved.

The other issue is that their loading dock is not secure from a truck perspective...you need to have a spotter to keep an eye on your truck or lock it between each load...anyone could wander over from the nearby train tracks or road.  It's not a problem if you're prepared with a lock or spotter, just be aware.

Inside the facility is secure.  My unit felt very secure  inside the facility and protected from the elements.</review>

(WARNING) Property management recently elected to host an array of 5G digital wireless network transmitters, mounted directly in my face, and elsewhere on the top floors perimeter, and since the place has been turned into a literal microwave drumhead.

Since the arrays have been operational I have been experiencing very low energy levels and find myself sleeping 4 or 5 hours more than normal, I never used to take naps but maybe once in a blue moon and last few weeks I have been needing a mid day Afternoon nap almost every day.      So I bought an Ev/RF monitor last week and it has confirmed hazardous levels are present throughout the residential portion of the complex.

I am not the only one who feels the 5G arrays are an issue here and possible public health concern for the community at large.  The interference is being recognized in several ways more than one.

I recently had the opportunity to dine at Tampa Garden Chinese Delight. Parking was a bit tight due to the business surround the restaurant, but there is a lot of street parking after 7pm. If you dare ;)
The location isn't very big, maybe 7 tables inside with no seating outside. Can't eat on a sidewalk!! There are however 2 large round tables that can seat parties of 6 with ease. BUT the table will become crowded if you order too many dishes. (We had maybe 6 different dishes and the table was packed!)
The portions are very generous. The food is flavorful. As a non meat eater, I had no issue finding food to eat here.

At the time I visited, they only accepted cash because their atm / credit card reader wasn't working. Not sure for how long, so bring cash or call to check on their payment options beforehand.<//review>

1497511211365<//date>
<Rate>5<//Rate>< text>
I love this place.  It's authentic Chinese fare that you can get right here in the Valley instead of flying across the Pacific Ocean!  Yes, the service is slow.  Yes, the decor is no frills.  But all that add to its authenticity.  It's pretty much family operated and they are desperately in need of better help.  But good help are hard to find in the restaurant business.  When you get there, don't worry about seating yourself.  Don't go when you are in a rush.  Just relax and enjoy the anticipation of yummy food that will be coming your way.  Their cares are in the preparation of the food, not pampering you and that suits me just fine.  The proprietor (I assume 'mum' of the family) is always friendly.  Always wants to feed us with her freshly hand made items.  And if she suggest to you to order something, do it.  She knows better than you what is good at her place!  Price is great.  Always order the XLB, the onion (pan) cake if it's not sold out for the day already.  I have not had a dish there that I don't like and I go there for lunch often because it is near work and have tried just about everything on the menu.<//text>

<rating>5</rating><text>I'm a dumpling fan. I'm a Taiwanese food fan. I'm a Szechuan food fan. I'm also a Dong Bei (Northeast China) food fan. This place pleases me because it has it all! Whenever craving hits, this is always our go-to spot in the valley.

Soup dumplings AKA XLB (Xiao Long Bao) - 8 pieces. The dumpling skin was perfect and not too chewy like Din Dai Fung. Size was on the normal side but it's OK because the reasonable price makes up for it. Filling was adequate, meaty, juicy, and sweet. (I like it sweet).

Pork and chive dumplings - 10 pieces. The dumpling skin was firm and dense, good texture for the mouth. Size was ginormous. Filling was plump, meaty, and very fulfilling.

Those baskets of joy were there to please! We ordered them to pair with our Beef Lomein entree. The portion was great! I like the generosity. Topped with tons of bean sprouts and beef. I like the wok-char taste to it therefore it's awesome for me. Best of all, no MSG.

The lady is nice and always made me feel like home. This hole-in-the-wall is real and they're on the right track. I'll definitely keep them in mind whenever I need a fix. Well recommended to all ages, race and culture.</text>< Pics>

<review>Do you want dumplings? There are franchise out in glendale.. that say they are good, but they are just too busy and the food is just way too sloppy. The wait lines are long and the taste just is bland. Tampa Garden Chinese Delight is the place to go for dumplings. Most of the Chinese students form CSUN will come here. The majority of patrons are Chinese, Caucasian and Hispanics. Usually on a weekend, tons of chinese people eat here. That should say something if Chinese people eat here. That means this is a legit place to try some dumplings. They have all kinds of dumplings: Chive, Lamb, Pork, etc. It just doesn't get any better. There's only one Tampa Garden Chinese Delight and it's in the heart of northridge. It's opened by a husband and wife and grandma. The grandma takes joy every morning and night making the dumplings. Her workspace is quite adequate and you can see her if she does it. That shows you How fresh these dumplings are. She uses fresh ingredients as well. The husband does the deliveries when needed and the wife does some of the cooking with a bit of help too. Otherwise the husband does the majority of the cooking. Food takes a while to make, since the staff is pretty small, but well worth it. better order some drinks! It's not ur average restaurant will full blown a/c. But hey, if you want superb food, I would do anything for that. Besides the dumpling I love to order the hand made beef noodle soup. A popular noodle soup with brisket which is popular in china. For those who have a hard time waiting, tampa garden chinese delight has a website where you can order online either for pickup.. or when u arrive, the food is ready to serve. I usually do that, to avoid the wait. Luckily this place is the only place that gives a great deal on dumplings and I don't have to drive all the way to alhambra for some dumplings. It also saves me the time to steam and fry them at home. Definitely a must-have to try for dumplings. You should friend me if u want to try these unique places. Hope u enjoyed this review.<//review>< response>

Great hike. My wife and I with two kids under five did this hike 45 years ago. I am 75 years old now and was curious to see how much change has taken place. < Rating>
5</Rating>
< review>
A jewel in the hills of Hollywood.
There are some hotels that feel alive and tell a story to the guest lucky enough to stay; This is one of those hotels. A journey back into a time when things were fun, a feeling of moving forward and immediately present is displayed upon entering this sleek unpretentious hidden hotel. The professional staff from valet, doorman, reception and housekeeping that always greet you w/a sincere smile - never saccharine.  It's an older hotel that has kept itself clean and polished over the years and has updated itself appropriately, and tastefully. The lush gardens are beautiful and beckon you to stroll before or after a lovely dinner at Cavatina. A wondefully romantic restaurant w/a well thought out wine list.
The cuisine prepared by Luis Morales is fresh, bright and bursting w/subtle nuances and the staff in the restaurant are more than accommodating. There is a levity that is pervasive on the grounds w/an abundance of rock and roll photography and paraphernalia.  This hotel might be in the heart of Hollywood but feels like an oasis w/twinkling fairy lights and a calm hush over a private retreat. The two pools are clean, cool and deep....I'm six foot two inches and despise these kiddie pools so many hotels favor presently. The large absorbent towels provided at poolside is a major plus and a detail often overlooked by many. The limited poolside menu  had options for all types of appetites. My family and I look forward to our return soon. Thank you to the entire staff at the Sunset Marquis, sorry this review is 6 months old but the heartfelt feelings are still on point. A special thanks to Yoman for providing such wonderful hospitality.< /review>

< rating>
4<//rating>
<Review>My wife and I spent five nights at Sunset Marquis and we really enjoyed our stay. The hotel room was large, with a really comfy bed and amazing walk in shower. Our room also had a large adjoining balcony, which was useful for afternoon drinks, overlooking the pool, and the occasional afternoon siesta.
We stayed from Monday to Saturday, so the atmosphere at the pool was pretty quiet during the week days and nights, however I assume, based on the Friday night and Saturday morning, that the atmosphere is a lot better on the weekend - perhaps making one's stay even more fun.
There was a slight problem upon check-out, where the valet charged us for three nights, rather than the actual one. (I wonder if this was intentional, to see if we wouldn't notice). However, this was rectified immediately.
The front counter staff were terrific. Our flight out of LA was not til midnight, and checkout was at midday. They took our bags and kept them securely, allowing us to explore the city for the next several hours, and come back and chill by the pool until it was time to go to the airport.
I'd definitely recommend this hotel to couples of families looking to have a fun and relaxing time in West Hollywood. The hotel is beautiful, and the room is comfortable. It is a bit on the pricey side, but hey - it's Hollywood!</Review>< Resp>

</record></dataset><record>
< Text>
A very tranquil quiet zen place in the heart of Sunset Strip. You will be whisked away by several things: the beautiful green landscaping, the black and white photographs of the legends of music and acting who have dined or stayed there and the serenity and quiet.

There are numerous comfortable sitting areas throughout the hotel, as well as benches placed in garden areas. It was wonderful to be able to sit and enjoy the beauty of it all, and close my eyes to hear the trickling fountains - without the noise of traffic or other city distractions.

The restaurant, Cavatina, is an indoor outdoor dining establishment. Be sure to check out the photo at the entrance of the restroom - I found it quite humorous :-) Food and service excellent. There is a lounge by the pool and and the entrance (Bar 1200), as well as a small cocktail area at the restaurant. And, there is a spa!

This hotel is not located on main road of this area. It is at the end of cul de sac surrounded by several luxury apartment houses, accordingly a "hidden gem". There is a rich history here; the hotel has undergone a number of changes since 1970s party days, and some of the history is evident by their "wall of fame"! Be sure to check out Morrison Gallery, which has rotating exhibits on various musicians.

I look forward to my next visit! Excellent service, I felt like a VIP from moment I entered to the time I left - worth every dime for the tranquil zen feeling!< /Text>

< name>
Bower Louber< /name>
< review>
I went over to the Sunset Marquis last night to catch up with some old friends that where in town for a few days from Florida. My friend was very excited that she got her picture taken with Steven Tyler the night before and she told me that I would love the place.

I was on my motorcycle so I didnt have to deal with the valet parking / lack of street parking fiasco that all car drivers have to deal with so I cruised right up and parked up front. I found my friends in the back at the restaurant bar and they started to take me for a tour.

This is a high end rock n roll hotel through and through. There is a recording studio on the facility called NightBird Recording Studios. Some heavy stuff has gone down here at the studios and here are a few artists that have recorded here.

Aerosmith
Billy Idol
Dave Navarro
Elton John
Gene Simmons
George Clinton
Heart
Madonna
Phil Collins
Ozzy Osbourne ... and that is just a few of the names.

I walked around and checked out both of the pools and checked out some of the nice villas. This place is really high end and is within walking distance of the Sunset strip. Very Cool!

We had a few cocktails at the bar downstairs and they played tons of old 70s rock which was awesome and it was loud! The place reaked of Nag Champa which was also a nice touch.</review>
</record>
</dataset><record>
